Backup\",\"topic\":\"bookmarks\",\"updated_by\":null,\"updated\":\"2019-05-27T18:34:47Z\"},{\"answers\":[],\"content\":\"<p>Since the \\\"add on\\\" issue with FireFox Moxilla a few weeks back, the \\\"save\\\" buttons (both in the browser, which is an add on; and on their website, which is not any type of browser add-on or extension) stopped appearing.  All of the pinterest emails are not clickable to save a pin.  Website auto \\\"pin this\\\" buttons are not working.  An update didn't work.  Clearing cookies, cache, temp history, etc. didn't work.  This happened specifically after the issues Moxilla had with firefox add-ons/extensions which was fixed so quickly most people didn't even know it happened.   When I visit <a href=\\\"http://Pinterest.com\\\" rel=\\\"nofollow\\\">Pinterest.com<\\/a> the page loads the header, but the rest of the page is blank.
